<div id="review_1260678352" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1260678352" />
    <a title="Beth" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9693189-beth"><img alt="Beth" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1338888456p2/9693189.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1260678352?book_show_action=true">Apr 21, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Beth" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Beth" href="/user/show/9693189-beth">Beth</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1260678352" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer204839969110672029">I thoroughly enjoyed this book and was very satisfied when I finished it. My favourite character was definitely Gecko and I felt really sorry for him towards the end locked in his s'hack. I loved the way Luna kept being constantly drawn to him while in the void and the twists and turns of the story were brilliant. When you see at the start how different Luna is from the rest of her family, especially her Dad, you really want her to succeed and overcome her difficulties with her school and Stepmo</span>
  <span id="freeText204839969110672029" style="display:none">I thoroughly enjoyed this book and was very satisfied when I finished it. My favourite character was definitely Gecko and I felt really sorry for him towards the end locked in his s'hack. I loved the way Luna kept being constantly drawn to him while in the void and the twists and turns of the story were brilliant. When you see at the start how different Luna is from the rest of her family, especially her Dad, you really want her to succeed and overcome her difficulties with her school and Stepmother. You find yourself wanting to find out more about her Mother and really feel for her when she goes through what she does with her Nanna. The story is quite complex at times but it is so fast-paced and gripping! There are characters introduced throughout the story whom you just completely mistrust and others who you immediately root for. The most intriguing parts of the book and most thrilling for me were when Luna is in both realities at once - online but still aware of the room around her, especially when she notices people in the room thinking she is still completely plugged in. There were times when I wanted to shout at the book because you just know that something bad is going to happen but you can't stop it. I loved the Slated virtual game world with the Lorders and Slateds.<br />I am passing this book straight on to another reader on Monday because I just loved it and have to share it! </span>
  <a data-text-id="204839969110672029" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('hHnUutUIMqb4HXcjTR1fIpZaFPFWhqHNAXMyCKo13wexmjtt8BSV7ZUj8jzJyPbhDdKv81b3iYeVrOJc0D7Dww==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('ACXLawZJEdp+c9o2IWxkNtSOxg6aXyLeCFG14XKFI/M1xiS8I1W2kRNNXymluc31TwZ9DJouCpScjmW1CI4/Nw==')})
  }
//]]>

<span id="freeTextContainer8856025009503539716">Teri has lived in France, Canada, Australia and England at more addresses than she can count, acquiring three degrees, a selection of passports and a silly name along the way. Past careers have included scientist, lawyer, optometrist, and, in England, various jobs in schools, libraries and an audiobook charity. The footpaths and canal ways of the Buckinghamshire Chilterns where she now lives inspi</span>
  <span id="freeText8856025009503539716" style="display:none">Teri has lived in France, Canada, Australia and England at more addresses than she can count, acquiring three degrees, a selection of passports and a silly name along the way. Past careers have included scientist, lawyer, optometrist, and, in England, various jobs in schools, libraries and an audiobook charity. The footpaths and canal ways of the Buckinghamshire Chilterns where she now lives inspired much of the setting of Slated. She hates broccoli, likes cats, and has finally worked out what she wants to do when she grows up.<br /><br />Facebook fan page: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.facebook.com/TeriTerryAuthor">http://www.facebook.com/TeriTerryAuthor</a><br />Notes from the Slushpile: group blog on writing for children <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://notesfromtheslushpile.blogspot.co.uk/">http://notesfromtheslushpile.blogspot...</a><br /><br />**IMPORTANT: Please do not message me on Goodreads with requests for review copies, swag, interviews, or anything else. See the contact section of my website for that. Messages on Goodreads may (and probably will) go unanswered!**</span>
